msg:The hotel is in a prime location, with ample parking spaces and easy access. You can see the river view from the window, and there will be a light show during the May Day holiday. The hotel service level needs to be improved, and the service is somewhat chaotic. For example, the room type and customer needs should be communicated in advance, or reminded in advance to arrive at 7 or 8 pm. I asked to arrange a room on the same floor, but after being told that there was no room, I arranged three rooms on different floors that were not adjacent to each other. Not only was it inconvenient to take care of the elderly, but the communication was delayed for a long time. It was difficult to eat dinner in Ningbo after 9 o'clock. In the end, the elderly and children could only eat takeout. The hotel air conditioner is a central air conditioner that can only blow cold air, not heat. The room is the last room on the side, with many windows, and it is very cold. The waiter said to bring a hot fan to solve it. The room design is a little less humane, such as the toilet is not smart, the TV is on the side of the window, it is biased to one side, not centered, and there is no mobile phone tray in the bathroom, no clothesline in the shower room, and no hooks. There is no place to put the clothes for bathing. The bathroom floor tiles are very slippery, and the child almost fell. The hair dryer is also very old, and the toilet paper is single-layer and very thin, which does not meet the five-star standard. It is recommended that those who have requirements for the room should ask about the room location and room type in advance. Communicate in advance. Thanks to the duty manager for his active communication and coordination. Although we did not live in a satisfactory room, we also helped us change the room so that the elderly would not live at the elevator entrance. Evening milk was prepared for the elderly. When leaving the hotel, it was thoughtful and meticulous, and xylitol biscuits were prepared for the elderly with diabetes. I hope the service will be improved in the future.

There are Heyi Avenue Shopping Center and Tianyi Square for shopping. There is 1844 Square next to entertainment. It is 2 kilometers away from the hotel to visit attractions. Tianyi Pavilion, Yuehu Park, and Drum Tower are really convenient. Let's talk about the hotel's services. The weather was very good on the day I went there. The concierge Xiao Ding at the door of the car was very enthusiastic to help me take down my luggage and took me to the lobby to guide me to check in. When checking in, the receptionist Lily saw that I was very hot and had small beads of sweat on my forehead, so she gave me tissues and mineral water. The front desk checked in quickly. Seeing that I was afraid of heat, she specially notified the room to send a cold air machine. When I was waiting for the elevator on the first floor, Lily introduced me to the coffee shop breakfast place and breakfast time. When I arrived in the room, she introduced the room facilities, the use of hotel wifi, and if there were any problems, I could call the room landline to have a hotline center to introduce its services in great detail. Now there are very few concierges who can patiently help guests introduce so much. When I came out the next day, I met Xiao Ding at the door again. He recommended a more distinctive restaurant in Ningbo for me when I went to a dinner party with friends. The sky was a bit cloudy at that time, so he brought me an umbrella in case of emergency. I have to say that the service was warm and proactive, and they were sincere and paid attention to details for the guests. In an environment where the five-star hotel market is flooded with people, I hope that domestic hotels can learn from Marriott to stick to the bottom line and improve the quality of service.

msg:I stayed at Ningbo Marriott for 3 nights in a row, and I am quite satisfied in all aspects. I should choose here next time. Briefly describe the advantages and disadvantages of each aspect:
Room:
1. Because I arrived late, the room type I booked is no longer available. I upgraded the suite for free. The room is relatively large and I live very comfortably. Thank you Amy at the front desk.
2. The bed is very comfortable, but I still hope to expand it to 2 meters in the future. After all, the house price is more than 1,000, and the width is 1.8 meters. 2 adults and a 5-year-old baby are crowded.
3. The decoration style is more conservative, not fashionable and young enough, more business-like, and quite satisfactory
4. I gave 4 bottles of water on the first day, 5 bottles on the second day, and 6 bottles on the last day. This is highly praised. There is no need to buy water during the tour.
5. I didn't find the hotel's razor before I went out in the morning. No one delivered it within 30 minutes after the call, so I had to go out to eat first.

breakfast:
1. There are both Chinese and Western breakfasts, and they are relatively rich, but they are basically the same every day for 3 days, and there is nothing new.
2. The noodles are delicious, the soup base is good, and there is also a Lantern Festival for breakfast

Pool:
The swimming pool is divided into large and small pools. The water in the big pool is relatively clean, but the water temperature is relatively low. It is not suitable for children after the National Day has cooled down. The water temperature in the small pond is too high, at least 40 degrees, similar to the bathhouse. Children will come up after playing in it for ten minutes, and adults will not be able to stay in it.

other:
1. The hotel is located in Sanjiangkou, the location is quiet, but it is said that the night view is not as good as a certain fragrance next to it
2. The hotel entrance of the underground parking lot is like a maze, and it also passes through the canteen of Marriott employees
3. After the license plate is registered, it will only be automatically recognized as a hotel guest on the first day. On the second and third days, the master of the security booth will be required to manually check before it is released.
